\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arc_8c_source_l00110}00110\ \ \ \ \ dy\ =\ arc-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_emb_arc___ac19242fe9e53942be61574685fbd49ed}{end}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_emb_vector___ac696d7e3434ae029d180ef550e61af2d}{y}}\ -\/\ arc-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_emb_arc___ad61a9cd980182f7b946d1a38aaee8562}{start}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_emb_vector___ac696d7e3434ae029d180ef550e61af2d}{y}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arc_8c_source_l00111}00111\ \ \ \ \ *chord\ =\ sqrt(dx*dx\ +\ dy*dy);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arc_8c_source_l00114}00114\ \ \ \ \ *radius\ =\ fabs(*chord\ /\ (2.0\ *\ sin(incAngleInRadians\ /\ 2.0)));}
